 jaanch ke baad ai report behad hairaan karne vaali he lagbhag sabhiashramonmen baari kamiyaan pai gayi
 The ashrams examined include Village Industries Institute Pratapgarh, Jagriti Ashtabhuja Nagar Pratapgarh, Ayesha Village Industries Hardoi, Jan Kalyan Samiti Lucknow, Awadh Rural Development Institute Dhammaur Sultanpur, Priyadarshini Child Home Special Adoption Agency Lucknow, and Awadh Rural Development Institute Sultanpur
 jaankaree ke mutabik, jaanch ke baad jo log isamen doshi paae gaye hai, unako diya gaya anudaan waapas liya jayega
 Also all kinds of help have been stopped with immediate effect
 aashray grihon kii badahaali dekhakar sarkaar ne faisla kiya he ki ashram main rahane valimahilaonka har 2 maheene par swasthya pareekshan karaayaa jayega
 The officers have been ordered that CCTV footage should be monitored in the DPO office
 16 se 18 varsh kii sabhi sanvasiniyon ko rojgaar se jodne ke liye kaushal vikaas prashikshan dilaane ke liye aadesh die gaye hai
 The NITI Aayog has recommended the PMO and HRD ministry to allow the opening of campuses of foreign universities in India
 ek report ke mutabik niti ayog ne us prastaav ko manjuuri de di he jisamen yah kaha gaya he ki desh main hair ajukeshan kii sthiti sudhaarney ke liye videshi uniwarsities ke campus kholane jaruri hai
 Let me tell you that when the UPA government brought this proposal, it was opposed by the BJP
 niti ayog ne piemo or echaradi ministry ko ek report saunpi he, jisamen videshi uniwarsities ke campus bharat main kholane kii baat kahi gai he
 The UGC Act will also be amended to invite foreign universities to India
 pichley saal, pradhanmantri narendra modi ne niti ayog se videshi uniwarsities ke campus kii sthapana karne se jude report ko study karne ko kaha tha
 In June 2015, senior bureaucrats were also called for a meeting to discuss this
 darasal yah vishay sarkaar ke nae ajukeshan policy kaa mukhya hissaa he
 With the help of opener Tillakaratne Dilshan's half-century, Sri Lanka thrashed Afghanistan captain Asghar Stanikzai's half-century to win the Group One match of the ICC World T20 Super 10 by six wickets today
 afghanistan ke 154 ran ke lakshya kaa peechha karte hue srilanka ne dilashaan kii 56 gend main teen chhakkon or aath chaukon kii madad se kheli naabad 83 ran kii pari kii badaulat 18
 Won 155 runs for four wickets in 5 overs
 unhone captain angelo maithyuj (10 gend main naabad 21) ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 3
 The unbroken partnership of 42 runs in 4 overs ensured the team's victory
 isse pehle afghanistan ne asagar (62) ke kariyar kii sarvshereshth pari or samiullah shenavari (31) ke saath paanchaven wicket ke liye 5
 Their partnership of 61 runs in 3 overs led to a challenging score of 153 for seven wickets
 asagar ne 47 gend kii apni pari main chaar chakke or teen chauke maare
 Chasing the target, Sri Lanka got off to a good start by adding 41 runs for the first wicket by Dilshan and Dinesh Chandimal (18)
 chandimal ne kareem sadik ke pehle over kii lagaataar gendon par chaukaa or chakka jadaa
 Dilshan also hit fast bowler Davalt Jadaran for two consecutive sixes
 chandimal haalanki aaf spinner mohammad nabi (25 ran par ek wicket) kii gend ko aage badhkar khilne kii koshish main midwicket par samiullah ko kaich de baithe
 Dilshan kept his stance
 unhone tej gendbaaj hamid hasan par lagaataar do chauke jadne ke baad nabi par chauke ke saath aathven over main team ke ranon kaa ardhashatak puraa kiya
 Lahiru Thirimane (06) hit a four off Rashid Khan (one wicket for 27 runs) but played the same leg-spinner for wickets
 tishaara perera (12) ne of spinner kareem par chakka jadaa lekin iske baad tej ran lene kii koshish main wicketiper mohammad shahzad ne unhen ran out kar diya jisase team kaa score teen wicket par 85 ran ho gaya
 Dilshan hit leg-spinner Samiullah Shenwari for four and then scored a half-century off 37 balls with a single
 srilanka ke ranon kaa shatak 15wein over main puraa hua
 In this over of Hamid, Dilshan hit a six while Chamara Kapugedara hit a four
 srilanka ko antim paanch over main jeet ke liye 41 ran kii darkaar thi
 Kapugedara (10) was run out by Dilshan's direct shot on the first ball in the next over from Nabi when the ball hit the wicket with the bowler's hand and the batsman was out of the crease
 captain maithyuj ne iske baad raashid par chakke or chauke ke saath gend or ranon ke bich ke antar ko kam kiya
 He also hit two consecutive fours at Davlat
 srilanka ko antim do over main 11 ran chahie the or dilashaan ne hamid par do chauke jadkar team ko jeet dilaa di
 Earlier, Asghar won the toss and decided to bat first but Mohammad Shehzad (08) got an easy catch to Dushmanta Chameera off Angelo Mathews in the third over
 salaami ballebaaj nur ali jaadaraan (20) or captain asagar ne duusare wicket ke liye 32 ran jodakar pari ko sanbhaalane kii koshish kii
 Both took the team's score to 36 for one wicket in the power play
 of spinner rangana herath ne nur ali ko bold karke afghanistan ko doosraa jhatka diya
 Tishara Perera then had Karim Sadiq (00) match the wicket-keeper Chandimal while Herath trapped Nabi (03) for Afghanistan, scoring 51 for four in 11 overs
 ran gati badhaane kaa jimmaa captain asagar ne sambhala
 He hit two sixes in a row over left-arm spinner Milinda Sriwardene
 samiullah ne bhi perera par chaukaa maaraa
 Asghar and Sameullah then hit Herath for sixes
 asagar ke chakke par haalanki thirimane ne midwicket boundry par kaich tapakaaya
 Sameullah completed a hundred of the team's runs in the 16th over with two consecutive fours over Perera
 samiullah ne agle over main kulshekhara par bhi chakka jadaa lekin agali gend par is shot ko dohraane kii koshish main long of par perera ko kaich de baithe
 He hit three fours and two sixes in his 14-ball innings
 kulshekhara kii agali gend par maithyuj ne cover main asagar kaa aasaan kaich tapakaaya
 Asghar completed the third half-century off 42 balls with a single off Chamira
 asagar ne 19wein over main perera par apana chauthaa chakka or phir chaukaa jadaa lekin antim gend par chandimal ko kaich de baithe
 Najibullah Jadran (12 not out from three balls) brought the team's score to 150 with sixes and fours off consecutive balls in Kulasekara's final over
 afghanistan ne antim nau over main tabadatod ballebaaji karte hue 102 ran jutaaye
 The comments srilanka kii ore se perera ne 33 ran dekar teen jabaki herath ne 24 ran dekar do wicket hasil kiye
 Kulasekara took 43 runs in four overs and got one wicket
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he

 dilashaan ne apane tevar barkaraar rakhe
 He completed the half-century of the team's runs in the eighth over with fours on Nabi after hitting two consecutive fours on fast bowler Hamid Hasan
 lahiru thirimane (06) ne raashid khan (27 ran par ek wicket) par chaukaa jadaa lekin isi leg spinner kii gend ko viketon par khel gaye
 Tishara Perera (12) hit a six off off-spinner Karim but then he was run out by wicketkeeper Mohammad Shahzad in an attempt to take a quick run which put the team's score at 85 for three
 dilashaan ne leg spinner samiullah shenavari par chaukaa or phir ek ran ke saath 37 gend main ardhashatak puraa kiya
 Sri Lanka's century of runs was completed in the 15th over
 hamid ke isi over main dilashaan ne chakka jadaa jabaki chamra kapugedara ne chaukaa maaraa
 Sri Lanka needed 41 runs to win in the last five overs
 nabi ke agle over main pehali gend par dilashaan ke sidhe shot par kapugedara (10) ran out ho gaye jab gendbaaj ke haath se chhukar gend viketon se takaraa gai or ballebaaj krij se baahar tha
 Captain Mathews then reduced the gap between the ball and the runs with sixes and fours on Rashid
 unhone dawlat par lagaataar do chauke bhi jade
 Sri Lanka needed 11 runs in the last two overs and Dilshan smashed Hamid with two fours to give the team victory
 isse pehle asagar ne toss jitkar pehle ballebaaji karne kaa faisla kiya lekin mohammad shahzad (08) tisare over main hi angelo maithyuj kii gend par dushmanta chamira ko aasaan kaich de baithe
 Opener Noor Ali Jadran (20) and captain Asgar tried to handle the innings by adding 32 runs for the second wicket
 donon ne power play main team kaa score ek wicket par 36 ran tak pahunchaaya
 Off-spinner Rangana Herath gave Afghanistan the second blow by bowling Noor Ali
 tishaara perera ne iske baad kareem sadik (00) ko wicketiper chandimal ke haathon match karaayaa jabaki herath ne nabi (03) ko pagabaadha karke 11 over main afghanistan kaa score chaar wicket 51 ran kiya
 Captain Asghar handled the task of increasing the run pace
 unhone baayen haath ke spinner milinda shrivardhane par lagaataar do chakke jade
 Samiullah also hit Perera
 asagar or samiullah ne iske baad herath par chakke jade
 On Asgar's six, however, Thirimanne caught a catch at midwicket boundary
 samiullah ne perera par lagaataar do chaukon ke saath 16wein over main team ke ranon kaa saikadaa puraa kiya
 Sameullah also hit a six over Kulasekara in the next over but caught Perera at the launch off in an attempt to repeat the shot on the next ball
 unhone 14 gend kii apni pari main teen chauke or do chakke maare
 On the next ball of Kulasekara, Mathews dripped an easy catch of Asghar in the cover
 asagar ne chamira kii gend par ek ran ke saath 42 gend main teesraa ardhashatak puraa kiya
 Asghar hit his fourth six and then a four over Perera in the 19th over but was caught by Chandimal on the last ball
 najibullah jaadaraan (teen gend main naabad 12) ne kulshekhara ke antim over main lagaataar gendon par chakke or chauke ke saath team kaa score 150 ran ke paar pahunchaaya
 Afghanistan scored 102 runs batting in the last nine overs
 tippaniyan For Sri Lanka, Perera took three for 33 while Herath took two wickets for 24 runs
 kulshekhara ne chaar over main 43 ran lutaae or unhen ek wicket mila

 is feechar se ab kisi bhi yujar ko yah pataa lagane main madad milegi ki use mila hua massej bhejne vaale ne jenerate kiya he yaa kisi or ke massej ko hi forward kiya gaya he
 In recent times, many cases of spreading fake news and rumors were seen in the country through social media
 watsap bhadakaau massej or afvaahen failaane ko lekar vivaadon main ghira hua he
 After this, full-page advertisements were also given by whatsapp on Tuesday in major newspapers across the country
 company ne apane nae feechar ko lekar duniya bhar main press relies jari kii he
 It says that the whatsapp user will know which messages have been forwarded to him
 isse yujar ko ek-duusare ke saath or watsap group main baatcheet karne main aasaani hogi
 However, the question still remains as to what extent this step of whatsapp will put a stop on safecare News
 haalanki, is nai suvidha se yujar ko yah bhi pataa chalegaa ki uske dost yaa rishtedaar dwaara bheja gaya massej unhone likhakar bheja he yaa kahin or se aayaa he
 For this feature, the user has to keep an updated version of whatsapp in their smartphone
 (aise dikhegaa forvarded massej
 Photo- whatsapp Blog) The company said, 'whatsapp is very serious about your security
 ham aapako forward kiye gaye massej ko share karne se pehle ek baar sochane kii salaah dete hai
 To avoid forwarding this, you can report spam (wrong message) with one touch or block the person sending the message
 'haal hi main desh ke kai ilaakon main watsap par prasaarit 'baccha chori' kii juthi khabaron, afvaahon kii vajah se bheed ke peet-peet kar logon ko jaan se maar dene kii kai ghatnaayen hui hai
 Such incidents were seen in Gujarat, Maharashtra, Rajasthan, Uttar Pradesh
 is bare main pichley hafte soochna praudyogiki mantri ravi shankar prasad ne watsap se zyada jimmedaari sunishchit karne ko kaha tha
 He also said that if fake news is spread with the help of whatsapp, the government will not tolerate it
 fasebuk ke swaamitv vaale watsap ne mangalvaar ko apane vigyaapan main logon ko juthi khabaron se bachane kii salaah di thi
 In this advertisement, whatsapp has said, 'together we can remove the problem of fake news
